Surroundings: It is very close to Longchi Mountain Bicycle Park, and a half-day trip can be arranged.

In short, it was a perfect trip!

msg:Location: 10 minutes away from the highway, the resort is hidden and private.
Environment: I went there in spring and summer, the grass on the ground was green, and there were many flowers on the roadside in the hotel. Except for the afternoon when it was a little hot, after the sun went down, a family of three rented a small electric stove and blew along the lake.
The wind was still very comfortable. This artificial lake is amazing, the water is very clear, and the fish are very big. We booked a lake view room. From the balcony, the entire lake and the mountain view echoed, which was beautiful.
Service: There are pick-up points at each location inside the hotel. If you want to go anywhere, just say hello to the service staff. After a while, a special driver will pick you up with a shuttle bus. Every service staff can smile and say hello to you when they bump into you. I especially want to mention Ambassador Lu Zhonghua, who helped us arrange a more suitable room in advance before we checked in, and patiently helped us answer questions. I must give him a thumbs up here.
Food: The hotel's breakfast buffet is very rich, with all the food you can think of, and the taste is very good. The full-time restaurant is very convenient except that it is a little expensive. Of course, you can also choose Zhangchu Town, which is closer to the hotel, which also has food and drinks.

msg:I only arranged a stay at Hidden Dragon Valley Junlan for May Day, and I got a lot of surprises.
The hotel is located in a valley. The mountains are not high, but there are mountains and water in the view, which is very suitable for relaxing vacation.
When I entered the gate of the park, I saw a sentence [Love at sunrise and sunset], and I felt that the hotel's intention was good. The six-year-old child asked what a vacation was, and the large lawns and trees that came into view also made this vacation worthy of the name.
The whole check-in was also very smooth. Because the entire park is very large, the accommodation is divided into different areas. Check-in and rooms are not in the same building, but the staff are skilled in business, and the shuttle bus is almost available on call. Fifteen minutes later, we have arrived at our room.

We went to Happy Paradise in the afternoon. The children loved it. We only played one-third of the various facilities because we were timid, but he gave a very high evaluation. The water play facilities are not open yet. We should make an appoin**ent with friends to come again in summer.

There is one more thing worth mentioning this time. All the staff we met had a very good sense of service, were warm and friendly, answered all questions, and took the initiative to ask about the stay experience. The toiletries prepared for the children were also of very good quality. There was a gift for check-out, and small toys were given, saying that the children could play with them on the return bus. It was very considerate!

This trip was very satisfying. I am a lazy woman who rarely writes reviews, but this time I really want to write a serious review. Yinlonggu Junlan is the best parent-child hotel I have stayed in in Jiangsu.

posted:Posted April 7, 2024
msg:Advantages: The place is very large, the outdoor children's playground facilities are new and large, the green environment is good, and the breakfast road is not bad.

Disadvantages: The service is not up to par, and some facilities are not designed reasonably

1. Check in at the service center, not the regular main building lobby, and there is no service staff to inform in advance. I also waited for a long time at the front desk of the main building, and the staff was always on the phone.

2. Self-driving check-in, the service center and the main building are not on the same road, and there is no notification. It leads to running back and forth.

3. Because the venue is very large and the shuttle bus is dispatched in a mess, it took a long time to wait for one, and when there was a car that was not full at the service center, it was told to wait for the next one, which was too strange. There are cars coming and going, but they don't stop at the service center.

4. The bathroom door of the room opens outside, but there is no space under the door to put a floor mat towel, resulting in water at the door after washing, and the water that was not wiped dry caused me to slip.

5. If it is a parent-child hotel, there are no footstools and toilet seats for young children in the room, which is very inconvenient for children to wash their hands and brush their teeth.

Finally, let me talk about the price. The package I bought on Ctrip was 999+300=1299, which was not worth the price! When he arrived on the same day, the price was 980+, and the children's park on 4/6 in the children's package was free (if it was not free for guests staying in the hotel, then there would be no fun for parents and children)
It was dark in the park that night, and we couldn't camp the next day because it rained, so we had to give up the content of the package.
I don't want to go again.
